                   <div class="sqs-block-content">
                    <h3>
                     AUTHOR:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="http://sachagoldberger.com/" target="_blank">
                      sacha goldberger
                     </a>
                    </p>

                   <div class="sqs-block-content">
                    <h3>
                     TYPOLOGICAL CATEGORIES:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="http://www.thetreemag.com/diario?category=Art">
                      ART
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     SOCIOLOGICAL CATEGORIES:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="http://www.thetreemag.com/diario?category=Community">
                      COMMUNITY
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     EVOCATIVECATEGORIES:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="/diario?category=wow!">
                      WOW!
                     </a>
                    </p>

                <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1434716924383_183315">
                 <div class="sqs-block-content">
                  <p>
                   TXT:
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   What if Superman was born in the sixteenth century?
                   <br/>
                   And what if the Hulk was a Duke?
                   <br/>
                   How might Van Eyck have portrayed Snow White?
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Sachas discovery of these characters, which goes back to childhood, gave birth to a desire
                   <br/>
                   to re-appropriate them, to take them back to a time forming the cornerstone of modern western art. Sacha wants to confront these icons of American culture with contemporary painters of the Flemish school. The collection demonstrates the use of 17 century techniques counterpointing light and shadow to illustrate nobility and fragility of the super powerful of all times. It also invites you to celebrate the heroes of your childhood. These characters have become icons to reveal their humanity: tired of having to save the world without respite, promised to a destiny of endless immortality, forever trapped in their character.
                   <br/>
                   The superheroes often live their lives cloaked in anonymity. These portraits give them a chance to  fix  their narcissism denied. By the temporal disturbance they produce, these images allow us to discover, under the patina of time, an unexpected melancholy of those who are to be invincible.
                   <br/>
                   As science fiction meets history of art, time meets an inexhaustible desire for mythology which is within each of us.
                  </p>
                  <p class="text-align-right">
                   txt:
                   <a href="http://sachagoldberger.com/portfolio/?portfolio=family-portrait" target="_blank">
                    sacha goldberger
                   </a>
                  </p>
                  <h1>
                   RECENT ART
                  </h1>

                    <h3>
                     TYPOLOGICAL CATEGORIES:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="http://www.thetreemag.com/diario?category=Art">
                      ART
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     SOCIOLOGICAL CATEGORIES:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="http://www.thetreemag.com/diario?category=Community">
                      COMMUNITY
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     EVOCATIVECATEGORIES:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="/diario?category=Composition">
                      COMPOSITION
                     </a>
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1434388431842_294874">
                 <div class="sqs-block-content">
                  <h3>
                   TXT:
                  </h3>
                  <p>
                   Jiang Guo Fang () was born in April 27th 1951 Nanchang, Jiangxi. In 1978 graduated from China Central Academy of Fine ArtsThe oil painting department, school to teach. In 1979 Central Academy of Drama dance department, Central Academy of fine art in 1984 of Department of oil painting course learning, after graduation to return to teaching at the Central Academy of Drama, now Professor.
                  </p>
                  <p class="text-align-right">
                   txt:
                   <a href="http://www.tuttartpitturasculturapoesiamusica.com/2014/03/Jiang-Guo-Fang.html" target="_blank">
                    tuttartpitturasculturapoesiamusica
                   </a>
                  </p>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1434388431842_219898">
                 <div class="sqs-block-content">
                  <h1>

                   <div class="sqs-block-content">
                    <h3>
                     AUTORE:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     vari
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     ANNO:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     2012
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     LUOGO:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     vari
                    </p>

                    </h3>

                     images n.d.
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     FONTE:
                    </h3>
                    <p style="margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px">

                      boredpanda

                 <div class="col sqs-col-6 span-6">
                  <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-b3be042795e54fed2d98">
                   <div class="sqs-block-content">
                    <h3>
                     CATEGORIA TIPOLOGICA:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="/diario?category=Art">
                      ART
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     CATEGORIA SOCIOLOGICA:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="http://www.thetreemag.com/diario?category=Community">
                      COMMUNITY
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     CATEGORIA EVOCATIVA:
                    </h3>
                    <p>
                     <a href="/diario?category=wow!">
                      WOW!
                     </a>
                     ,
                     <a href="/diario?category=On-the-Road">
                      ON_THE_ROAD
                     </a>
                    </p>
                    <h3>
                     NOTE:
                    </h3>
                    <p style="margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px">
                    </p>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1418395783358_31503">
                 <div class="sqs-block-content">
                  <h3>
                   TXT:
                  </h3>
                  <p dir="ltr">
                   Questa serie di opere di street art non sono dello stesso autore e nemmeno collocate nel solito paese, la caratteristica che le accomuna  che sono nate utilizzando come punto di partenza dei soggetti presenti nella citt. Il tubo di scarico di un edificio diventa una grande cannuccia, una crepa nell'intonaco la corda di spider man,delle foglie su una parete nei capelli di una ragazza etc. La street art ha sempre avuto bisogno del tessuto cittadino per giustificare la propria esistenza ma in questo caso ha fatto un passo avanti, ha trasformato soggetti esistenti privi di ogni interesse nel fulcro dell'opera.
                  </p>
                  <p class="text-align-right" dir="ltr">
                   txt: progettospore
                  </p>
                  <p>
                  </p>
                  <h3>
                   RECENTI IN ARTE
                  </h3>

        <div class="site-info">
         <h3 class="site-title">
          The Tree mag
         </h3>
         <div class="site-description">
          <h3>
           This is what
           <strong>
            THE TREE
           </strong>
           is.
          </h3>
          <p>
           The Tree Magazine is built around categories we have chosen to name "fruit" and "trees".
          </p>
          <p>
           The Tree Magazine talks about contemporary design architecture. Our trees and fruits are the keys to a subjective interpretation of reality and the present.
          </p>
          <p>
           The Tree Magazine offers a fresh view on architecture that is in no way exhaustive or definitive.
          </p>
         </div>

The Tree Mag does not intend to publish any content that may be considered offensive. If you find that to be the case, please get in touch and we will be happy to remove it.
